    customer_id INT PRIMARY KEY,

);

);

    account_id INT REFERENCES Accounts(account_id),

    transaction_date TIMESTAMP
);

    customer_id INT PRIMARY KEY,

    account_id INT PRIMARY KEY,

CREATE TABLE Transactions (

    account_id INT REFERENCES Accounts(account_id),
    transaction_type VARCHAR(50),
    amount DECIMAL(10, 2),
    transaction_date TIMESTAMP
);
